function m(n,q,r,...)if not l then n=T()l=true end;local l={}r=r or o()local l=0;return(function(...)local o={}local s={...}local t={}local u={}local l=n[2][1][l]local v=-(1)local w=(y(R,...)-1)for l=0,w,1 do if(l>=n[6][1])then u[l-n[6][1]]=s[l+1]else o[l]=s[l+1]end end;local s=w-n[6][1]+1;while(true)do local w=l;l=w[6]local y=w[1]if(y<=38)then if(y<=18)then if(y<=8)then if(y<=3)then if(y<=1)then if(y==0)then local m=w[2]local n=o[m+2]local p=o[m]+n;o[m]=p;if(n>0)then if(p<=o[m+1])then l=w[3]o[m+3]=p end elseif(p>=o[m+1])then l=w[3]o[m+3]=p end elseif(y<=1)then local l=w[2]local m=o[w[3]]o[l+1]=m;o[l]=m[o[w[4]]]end elseif(y==2)then o[w[2]]=o[w[3]]*o[w[4]]elseif(y<=3)then local m=w[2]o[m]=0+(o[m])o[m+1]=0+(o[m+1])o[m+2]=0+(o[m+2])local n=o[m]local p=o[m+2]if(p>0)then
